The supported values for firmware component are 'ilo', 'cpld', 'power_pic', 'bios' and 'chassis'. The firmware images will be applied (in the order given) one by one on the baremetal server. For more information, see https://docs.openstack.org/ironic/latest/admin/drivers/ilo.html#initiating-firmware-update-as-manual-clean-step", 'required': True}}, 'interface': 'management'}] for interface management {{(pid=15286) __new__ /opt/stack/ironic/ironic/drivers/base.py:266}}
